25:T3934,<entryFree id="n14112" key="ذَهَبَ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">ذَهَبَ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, A, &amp;c.,) aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Ba" lang="ar">ذَهَبَ</orth>
                  </form>, (A, K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَابٌ</foreign> (S, A, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">ذِهَابٌ</foreign> (TA) and <foreign lang="ar">ذُهُوبٌ</foreign> (S, A, K) and <foreign lang="ar">مَذْهَبٌ</foreign>, (A, K,) <hi rend="ital">He</hi> (a man, S, [and a beast,]) <hi rend="ital">went</hi> [<hi rend="ital">in any manner,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">any pace</hi>]; <hi rend="ital">went,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">passed, along; marched; journeyed; proceeded: went,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">passed, away; departed:</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">مَشَى</foreign>, (A,) or <foreign lang="ar">سَارَ</foreign>, (K,) or <foreign lang="ar">مَرّ</foreign>: (S, A, K:) and said of a mark or trace or the like [as meaning <hi rend="ital">it went away</hi>]. (Msb.) [And hence, <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">It wasted away; became consumed, destroyed, exhausted, spent,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">expended.</hi>]          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ إِلَيْهِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He went, repaired, betook himself,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">had recourse, to him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it.</hi> (TA.) And they say also, <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ الشَّأْمَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He went to Syria</hi>]; making the verb trans. without a particle; for although <foreign lang="ar">الشأم</foreign> is here a special adv. n., they liken it to a vague locality. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ عَنْهُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, went from, quitted, relinquished,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">left, him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ فِىالأَرْضِ</foreign>, (A, Msb,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَابٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">ذُهُوبٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">مَذْهَبٌ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">He went away</hi> [<hi rend="ital">into the country,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">in the land</hi>]: (Msb:) [but it often means <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">he went into the open country,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">out of doors, to satisfy a want of nature:</hi> or simply] <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">he voided his excrement,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">ordure.</hi> (A.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ بِهِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He went,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">went away, with him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it:</hi> (A:) and <hi rend="ital">he made him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, to go, go away, pass away,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">depart;</hi> (A, Msb, K;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n14112-1" target="اذهبهُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, (S, A, Msb, K,) and <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n14112-2" target="اذهب" n="2" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>بِهِ</foreign>, (K,) but this is rare; (Zj, TA;) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n14112-3" target="ذهّبهُ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n14112"/></foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">تَذْهِيبٌ</foreign>: (MF:) [all may likewise be rendered <hi rend="ital">he removed, dispelled, put away,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">banished, it;</hi> properly and tropically: and <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">he made it to cease; made away with it, did away with it, made an end of it; wasted, consumed, destroyed, exhausted, spent,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">expended, it;</hi> and these meanings may perhaps be intended by <foreign lang="ar">أَزَالَهُ</foreign>, whereby the first is explained in the A and K, as are also the second and third in the K:] or, accord. to some, when <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ</foreign> is trans. by means of <foreign lang="ar">بِ</foreign>, accompaniment is necessarily signified; but not otherwise; so that if you say <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ بِهِ</foreign>, the meaning is, <hi rend="ital">he went away with him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it;</hi> i. e., <hi rend="ital">accompanying him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it;</hi> [<hi rend="ital">he took away,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">carried off</hi> or <hi rend="ital">away, him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it;</hi>] but if you say   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n14112-4" target="اذهبهُ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> or   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n14112-5" target="ذهّبهُ" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n14112"/></foreign>, the meaning is, <hi rend="ital">he made him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, to go, go away, pass away,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">depart, alone, without accompanying him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it:</hi> this, however, is not agreeable with the phrase in the Kur [ii. 16], <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ ٱللّٰهُ بِنُورِهِمْ</foreign> [though this may be well rendered <hi rend="ital">God taketh away their light</hi>]. (MF, TA.) [Hence,] one says, <foreign lang="ar">أَيْنَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">يُذْهَبُ بِكَ</foreign>, which may mean <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">Where,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">whither, wilt thou be taken away, and what will be done with thee and made to come to pass with thee,</hi> if this be thine intellect? or, accord. to Mtr, it is a saying of the people of Baghdád, addressed to him whom they charge with foolish judgment or opinion, as meaning <foreign lang="ar">أَيْنَ يُذْهَبُ بِعَقْلِكَ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">Where,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">whither, is thine intellect taken away?</hi>]. (Har p. 574.) [In like manner one says, <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ عَقْلُهُ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">His reason,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">intellect, quitted him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">forsook him; he became bereft of his reason,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">intellect.</hi> And <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ فُؤَادُهُ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">His heart forsook him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">failed him,</hi> by reason of fear or the like.] And <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ لَحْمُهُ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">His flesh wasted away</hi>]. (K in art. <foreign lang="ar">بحر</foreign>, &amp;c.) And <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ الرَّجُلُ فِى القَوْمِ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">The man became lost</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">he disappeared</hi>] <hi rend="ital">among the people,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">party.</hi> (A.) And <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ المَآءَ فِى اللَّبَنِ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">The water became lost</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">it disappeared</hi>] <hi rend="ital">in the milk.</hi> (A.)          <sense type="b" n="6">-b6-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ عَلَيْهِ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">It escaped his memory; he forgot it.</hi> (A, TA.) And <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">It was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, dubious, confused,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">vague, to him.</hi> (MA.)          <sense type="b" n="7">-b7-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ مَذْهَبًا حَسَنًا</foreign> (S, A, TA) <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">He pursued a good way, course, mode,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">manner, of acting</hi> or <hi rend="ital">conduct</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like.</hi> (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ فِى الدِّينِ مَذْهَبًا</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He formed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">held, an opinion,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a persuasion,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a belief, respecting religion:</hi> or, accord. to Es-Sarakustee, <hi rend="ital">he introduced an innovation in religion.</hi> (Msb.) And <foreign lang="ar">ذَهَبَ مَذْهَبَ فُلَانٍ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He pursued the way, course, mode,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">manner, of acting</hi> &amp;c. <hi rend="ital">of such a one.</hi> (Msb.)
